country_event = { #history
	id = qiedom.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiedom.1" }
	title = qiedom.1.t
	desc = qiedom.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_warlords

	is_triggered_only = yes #fired by history file
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = qiedom.1.a #Long Live the Emperor!
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = qiedom.2 
				days = 3 
			} 
		} # political parties
	}
}

country_event = { # death of wang chengbin
	id = qiedom.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiedom.4" }
	title = qiedom.4.t
	desc = qiedom.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_china_abandoned

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = qiedom.4.a #we need new leadership
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = QIE_leadership_crisis
			add_idea = QIE_leadership_crisis_bad
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 1177 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 1177 }
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #black monday
	id = qiedom.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiedom.5" }
	title = qiedom.5.t
	desc = qiedom.5.d
	picture = china_industry

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = qiedom.5.a #damn it!
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = QIE_black_monday
			days = 150
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = { #Shanxi Black Monday event
				country_event = { 
					id = shx.earlygame.11
					days = 2 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #assembly returns to normal
	id = qiedom.17
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiedom.17" }
	title = qiedom.17.t
	desc = qiedom.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_wu_peifu_time_cover

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = QIE_placate_NCERA
		has_country_flag = QIE_placate_YCP
		has_country_flag = QIE_placate_manchu
	}

	option = {
		name = qiedom.17.a #excellent
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = QIE_placate_NCERA
			clr_country_flag = QIE_placate_YCP
			clr_country_flag = QIE_placate_manchu
		}
		remove_ideas = QIE_outraged_parties
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = qiedom.19 #cao kun is removed for drunkenness
				days = 15
				random = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

		}
	}
}

country_event = { #chen tiaoyuan asks for help
	id = qielepcollapse.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qielepcollapse.7" }
	title = qielepcollapse.7.t
	desc = qielepcollapse.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ANQ_chen_tiaoyuan

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Wu promises support for Chen
		name = qielepcollapse.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_PRO_LEP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_COUP_FAILS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_COUP_FAILS_WU
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_MANCHU_COUP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ANQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = anq.3 #wu says yes
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
	}

	option = { #Wu says no, Chen goes to the Japanese
		name = qielepcollapse.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
					option = QIE_PRO_ANQ
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ANQ = {
				country_event = {
					id = anq.4
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.03

country_event = { #qi asks wu (if wu said no to chen), triggered from qielepcollapse.5
	id = qielepcollapse.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qielepcollapse.8" }
	title = qielepcollapse.8.t
	desc = qielepcollapse.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEP_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			ANQ = {
				has_country_flag = qing_supports_chen
			}
			has_country_flag = wu_intervenes_proANQ
		}
	}

	option = { #Give him support
		name = qielepcollapse.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 73
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_COUP_FAILS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_COUP_FAILS_WU
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_PRO_ANQ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_MANCHU_COUP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = QIE_wu_backs_qi
			LEP = {
				country_event = {
					id = qielepcollapse.9 #wu says yes
					days = 1
				}
			}
			#intervention choice will fire from Qi assuming control (lepcollapse.19)
		}
	}

	option = { #Wu says no, leads to coup
		name = qielepcollapse.8.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 27
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_PRO_LEP
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = QIE_LEP_PATH
						option = QIE_PRO_ANQ
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = QIE_not_backs_qi
		LEP = {
			country_event = {
				id = qielepcollapse.10
				days = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = LEP_REP_flag
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -150
		set_country_flag = wu_no_intervene
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = qielepcollapse.21 #widespread protests break out
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = qiefor.1 #beijing govt demands anqing submit
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiefor.1" }
	title = qiefor.1.t
	desc = qiefor.1.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = qiefor.1.a #submit - QIE is anti-concession if they go beijing coup route, ANQ should join if they are not in FNG sphere
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		QIE = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = no }
				create_faction = north_zhili_faction
				add_to_faction = ANQ
				set_country_flag = created_northern_zhili_faction
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				var:faction_leader = { add_to_faction = ANQ }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = ANQ
			}
			country_event = {
				id = qiefor.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = qiefor.1.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		QIE = {
			country_event = {
				id = qiefor.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_to_faction = LEP
				set_faction_name = "Zhili Clique"

				days = 1

		}
		QIE = {

			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = QIE }
		every_navy_leader = { set_nationality = QIE }
		FROM = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = QIE_integrating_province
				days = 90
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { QIE = { is_ai = yes } }
			QIE = { change_tag_from = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = qiefor.49.c #nah b

country_event = { #qing asks faction anqing before war
	id = qiefor.66
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiefor.66" }
	title = qiefor.66.t
	desc = qiefor.66.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = qiefor.66.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 7 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 6 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		custom_effect_tooltip = anq_increase_qie_3
		hidden_effect = {
			ANQ = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				ANQ_remove_beijing_spirit = yes
				ANQ_calculate_beijing_level = yes
				ANQ_add_beijing_spirit = yes
			}
		}
		QIE = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = no }
				create_faction = north_zhili_faction
				add_to_faction = ANQ
				set_country_flag = created_northern_zhili_faction
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				var:faction_leader = { add_to_faction = ANQ }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = ANQ
			}
			country_event = {
				id = qiefor.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = qiefor.66.b #no
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 10 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 7 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 6 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anq_decrease_cred_10
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = credibility_factor
			value = 10
		}
		anq_recalculate_chens_credibility = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = anq_decrease_qie_2
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.02
			}
			ANQ_remove_beijing_spirit = yes
			ANQ_calculate_beijing_level = yes
			ANQ_add_beijing_spirit = yes
		}
		ANQ_increase_beijing_anger_3x = yes
		QIE = {
			country_event = {
				id = qiefor.69
				days = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = QIE_anqing_refuses_before
		}
	}
}

	desc = {
		text = qiefor.75.d1
		trigger = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_large_progress } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = qiefor.75.d2
		trigger = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_progress } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = qiefor.75.d3
		trigger = {
			ANQ = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_large_progress
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_progress
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = qiefor.75.a
		trigger = {
			ANQ = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_large_progress
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_progress
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_large_progress } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = anq_increase_qie_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_progress } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = anq_increase_qie_1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = qiefor.75.b
		trigger = {
			ANQ = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_large_progress
					has_country_flag = ANQ_qie_conference_progress
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

	desc = qiefor.83.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = qiefor.83.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 7}
				add = 40
			}
			modifier = {
				date > 1941.1.1
				add = 30
			}
		}
		QIE = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				change_tag_from = ANQ
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = ANQ
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = QIE_united_anqing
			country_event = {
				id = qiefor.81
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = qiefor.83.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level > 7}
				add = -40
			}
			modifier = {
				date > 1941.1.1
				check_variable = { ANQ_beijing_level < 8}
				add = -30
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		ANQ_increase_beijing_anger_3x = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = anq_decrease_qie_5
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			ANQ_remove_beijing_spirit = yes
			ANQ_calculate_beijing_level = yes
			ANQ_add_beijing_spirit = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ANQ_refused_integration_qing_after } }
			QIE = {
				country_event = {
					id = qiefor.84
					days = 1
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ANQ_refused_integration_qing_after
		}
		else = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { #war goal
					id = qiefor.85
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			LEP = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = LEP_NAN }

					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes

				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 0
				radical_socialist = 0
				syndicalist = 0
				social_democrat = 6
				social_liberal = 3
				market_liberal = 8
				social_conservative = 5
				authoritarian_democrat = 46
				paternal_autocrat = 30
				national_populist = 2
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				QIE_Yan_Huiqing_hog_ade
				QIE_Bai_Jianwu_for_ade
				QIE_Xiong_Bingqi_eco_ade
				QIE_Zhang_Luao_sec_ade

				QIE_Wu_Peifu_carm
			}
			remove_ideas = QIE_fractured_empire
			set_country_flag = Aisin_Gioro_Zaifeng_dead
			set_country_flag = Aisin_Gioro_Jixing_dead
			set_country_flag = Aisin_Gioro_Zaixun_dead
			set_country_flag = Tong_Jixu_dead
		}
		remove_ideas = QIE_fractured_empire
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Manchu Cavalry Division" }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Manchu Imperial Guard" }

		country_event = {
			id = qiecoup.14
			days = 1
		}

			id = qiecoup.15
			days = 2
		}

			}

					modifier = KR_friendly
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SHX
					modifier = KR_friendly
				}
				SHX = { country_event = qiecoup.23 } #the coup succeeds! time to intervene
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = QIE_song_backs_coup
						has_country_flag = QIE_zhang_backs_coup

					SQI = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
					}

					modifier = KR_friendly
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SQI
					modifier = KR_friendly
				}

			}

				promote_leader = yes

					hours = 3
				}

country_event = {
	id = qiefocus.27 #qing asks for guarantee
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiefocus.27" }
	title = qiefocus.27.t
	desc = qiefocus.27.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = qiefocus.27.a #yes, we need an eastern bulwark
		give_guarantee = FROM
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		FROM = { give_military_access = ROOT }
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = GEA }
			FROM = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = non_aggression_pact
				}
				give_military_access = GEA
			}
			GEA = { give_military_access = FROM }
		}

			name = QIE_social_democrat_party_MZ
			long_name = QIE_social_democrat_party_MZ_long
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = QIE_ROC_H
		if = {
			limit = { 
				SZC = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SZC_A_Victory_From_Baoding
					}
				}
			}
			QIE_sichuan_comeback = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ANQ = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			QIE_wan_comeback = yes
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			QIE_huang_yan_pei_hog
			QIE_li_zhu_chen_for
			QIE_zhang_nai_qi_eco
			QIE_fu_liang_sec
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					CHI = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					country_event = {
						id = qiepan.43
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = qiehunluan.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event qiehunluan.1" }

	desc = qiehunluan.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes 
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = qiehunluan.1.a 
		set_cosmetic_tag = QIE_LIN
		load_focus_tree = { 
			tree = Qing_Lie
			keep_completed = yes 
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			QIE_huan_luan_de_yi_qie
			free_trade
			civilian_economy
			disarmed_nation
		}
		complete_national_focus = QIE_shi_liao_wei_ji
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SHX = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				SHX = {
					transfer_state = 607
					transfer_state = 799
					transfer_state = 1060
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					HNN = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				HNN = {
					transfer_state = 620
					transfer_state = 1048
				}
			}
			else = {
				var:613.owner = {
					transfer_state = 620
				}
			}
			var:613.owner = {
				transfer_state = 597
				transfer_state = 1059
				transfer_state = 1058
			}
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 0
				syndicalist = 0
				radical_socialist = 20
				social_democrat = 10
				social_liberal = 20
				market_liberal = 5
				social_conservative = 15
				authoritarian_democrat = 20
				paternal_autocrat = 5
				national_populist = 5
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name =  QIE_radical_socialist_party_jkh_long
				name =  QIE_radical_socialist_party_jkh
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name =  QIE_social_democrat_party_jkh_long
				name =  QIE_social_democrat_party_jkh
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name =  QIE_social_liberal_party_jkh_long
				name =  QIE_social_liberal_party_jkh
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name =  QIE_authoritarian_democrat_party_jkh_long
				name =  QIE_authoritarian_democrat_party_jkh
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name =  QIE_paternal_autocrat_party_jbl_long

		}
